Picasso represented himself ceaselessly throughout his long career, whether in a dashed-off pencil sketch, as a flourish at the bottom of a letter, or on a giant painted canvas.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAt the suggestion of Picasso’s widow Jacqueline, the distinguished art historian Pascal Bonafoux began studying Picasso’s self-portraits more than forty years ago. This meticulously researched book presents the fruits of his decades-long project. From the first self-portrait attributed to Picasso in 1894, when he was a thirteen-year-old boy, until his final self- portrait in 1972, a year before his death, Bonafoux charts the evolution of the artist’s life and art. Here is Picasso as a student; as a young bohemian; as an impetuous artist in Paris; as harlequin; as lover, husband, and father; and finally, as an old man confronting his mortality. này một cách điêu luyện hơn loạt tranh khắc gỗ mang tính bước ngoặt Ba mươi sáu cảnh núi Phú Sĩ của Katsushika Hokusai (1760–1849). Nhà in nổi tiếng ghi lại Nhật Bản thế kỷ 19 với nghệ thuật đặc biệt và sự ngưỡng mộ, tôn vinh vùng nông thôn, thành phố, con người và vẻ đẹp tự nhiên thanh bình. Được sản xuất ở đỉnh cao tham vọng nghệ thuật của Hokusai, bộ truyện là một tác phẩm tinh túy của ukiyo-e đã giúp nghệ sĩ được toàn thế giới công nhận là bậc thầy hàng đầu trong nghề của mình.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 class=\"h1\"\u003eIn the Footsteps of a Master\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"row read-more-content pb-2\"\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"col-12 col-lg-6 pb-4 pb-lg-0\"\u003e\n\u003ch5\u003eHokusai’s complete \u003cem\u003eViews of Mount Fuji\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/h5\u003e\nMount Fuji has long been \u003cstrong\u003ea centerpiece of  cultural imagination\u003c/strong\u003e, and nothing captures this with more virtuosity than the \u003cstrong\u003elandmark woodblock print series \u003cem\u003eThirty-six Views of Mount Fuji\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e by Katsushika Hokusai (1760–1849). The renowned printmaker documents 19th-century Japan with exceptional artistry and adoration, celebrating its countryside, cities, people, and serene natural beauty. Produced\u003cstrong\u003e at the peak of Hokusai’s artistic ambition\u003c/strong\u003e, the series is \u003cstrong\u003ea quintessential work of \u003cem\u003eukiyo-e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e that earned the artist world-wide recognition as a leading master of his craft.\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003eThe prints illustrate Hokusai’s own obsession with Mount Fuji as well as the flourishing domestic tourism of the late Edo period. Just as the mountain was a cherished view for travelers heading to the capital Edo (now Tokyo) along the Tōkaidō road, \u003cstrong\u003eMount Fuji is the infallible backdrop to each of the series’ unique scenes\u003c/strong\u003e. Hokusai captures the distinctive landscape and provincial charm of each setting with a \u003cstrong\u003evivid palette \u003c/strong\u003eand \u003cstrong\u003eexquisite detail\u003c/strong\u003e. Including the iconic \u003cem\u003eUnder the Great Wave off Kanagawa\u003c/em\u003e (also\u003cem\u003e The Great Wave\u003c/em\u003e), this widely celebrated series is \u003cstrong\u003ea treasure of international art history\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003eAmong only a few complete reprints of the series, this \u003cstrong\u003eXXL edition\u003c/strong\u003e pays homage to Hokusai’s striking colors and compositions with \u003cstrong\u003eunprecedented care and magnitude\u003c/strong\u003e. Bound in the Japanese tradition with \u003cstrong\u003euncut paper\u003c/strong\u003e, \u003cem\u003eThirty-six Views of Mount Fuji\u003c/em\u003e presents the original 36 plates plus the additional 10 later added by the artist. The perfect companion piece to TASCHEN’s \u003cem\u003eOne Hundred Views of Edo\u003c/em\u003e and \u003cem\u003eThe Sixty-Nine Stations along the Kisokaidō\u003c/em\u003e, this publication paints an enchanting picture of pre-industrial Japan and is itself\u003cstrong\u003e a stunning monument to the art of woodblock printing\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\u003cp\u003eGiá sản phẩm trên Tiki đã bao gồm thuế theo luật hiện hành. Bên cạnh đó, tuỳ vào loại sản phẩm, hình thức và địa chỉ giao hàng mà có thể phát sinh thêm chi phí khác như phí vận chuyển, phụ phí hàng cồng kềnh, thuế nhập khẩu (đối với đơn hàng giao từ nước ngoài có giá trị trên 1 triệu Today, Impressionism is close contender for the world’s favorite period of painting. With blockbuster exhibitions, record-breaking auction prices, and packed museums, the works once dismissed as unfinished or imprecise are now beloved for their atmospheric evocation of time and place, as well as the stylistic flair of rapid brushstrokes upon canvas.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eDespite its popularity and a whole host of publications, many areas and artists of Impressionism remain inadequately researched. class=\"h1\"\u003eSau khi Egon Schiele thoát khỏi cái bóng của người cố vấn và hình mẫu Gustav Klimt, ông chỉ có mười năm để khắc ghi phong cách đặc trưng của mình vào biên niên sử hiện đại trước khi Là một đứa trẻ thần đồng nhận thức khá rõ về thiên tài của mình và là một kẻ thích khiêu khích đầy đam mê, điều này không phải là một thử thách quá lớn.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"h1\"\u003eCác bức tranh và bản vẽ ghi lại thập kỷ màu mỡ cuối cùng trong cuộc đời của Schiele. Những tác phẩm này được đi kèm với các bài tiểu luận giới thiệu cuộc đời và tác phẩm của ông, đặt vị trí của bậc thầy người Áo trong bối cảnh của Chủ nghĩa Biểu hiện Châu Âu và lập biểu đồ về di sản phi thường của ông.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 class=\"h1\"\u003eTwisted Brilliance\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"row read-more-content pb-2\"\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"col-12 col-lg-6 pb-4 pb-lg-0\"\u003e\n\u003ch5\u003eObsessive, radical, disturbing: Egon Schiele\u003c/h5\u003e\nAfter \u003cstrong\u003eEgon Schiele\u003c/strong\u003e (1890–1918) freed himself from the shadow of his mentor and role model \u003cstrong\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e, he had just ten years to inscribe his signature style into the \u003cstrong\u003eannals of modernity\u003c/strong\u003e before the Spanish flu claimed his life. Being a child prodigy quite aware of his own genius and a \u003cstrong\u003epassionate provocateur\u003c/strong\u003e, this didn’t prove to be too big a challenge.\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003eHis \u003cstrong\u003ehaggard, overstretched figures\u003c/strong\u003e, \u003cstrong\u003eextreme depiction of sexuality\u003c/strong\u003e and \u003cstrong\u003eself-portraits,\u003c/strong\u003e in which he staged himself with emaciated facial expressions \u003cstrong\u003ebordering between brilliance and madness\u003c/strong\u003e, had none of the decorative quality of Klimt’s hymns of love, sexuality and yearning devotion. Instead, Schiele’s work spoke of a \u003cstrong\u003ebrutal honesty\u003c/strong\u003e, one that would upset and irreversibly change Viennese society.\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003eAlthough his works were later defamed as “degenerate” and for a time were almost forgotten altogether, they \u003cstrong\u003einfluenced generations of artists\u003c/strong\u003e—from \u003cstrong\u003eGünter Brus\u003c/strong\u003e and \u003cstrong\u003eFrancis Bacon\u003c/strong\u003e to \u003cstrong\u003eTracey Emin\u003c/strong\u003e. Today, his then misunderstood oeuvre continues to fetch exorbitant prices on the international art market.\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003eThis monograph, first published in an XL edition, is now available in a slightly abridged, more compact edition to celebrate TASCHEN’s  and features \u003cstrong\u003ethe paintings\u003c/strong\u003e and\u003cstrong\u003e drawings\u003c/strong\u003e that \u003cstrong\u003eretrace the fertile last decade of Schiele’s life\u003c/strong\u003e. These works are accompanied by essays introducing his life and oeuvre, situating the Austrian master in the context of European Expressionism and charting his extraordinary legacy.\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\u003cp\u003eGiá sản phẩm trên Tiki đã bao gồm thuế theo luật hiện hành. The fronds were a reference to his groundbreaking \u003cem\u003eNatural History of Palms: a work in three volumes\u003c/em\u003e, published between 1823 and 1853.\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003eThis encyclopedic treasury of \u003cstrong\u003e240 exquisite chromolithographic illustrations \u003c/strong\u003ewas based on von Martius’s expeditions through Brazil and Peru. From 1817 to 1820, he traveled over \u003cstrong\u003e2,250 km (1,400 miles) through the Amazon basin\u003c/strong\u003e to investigate natural history and native tribes with zoologist Johann Baptist von Spix.\u003cbr /\u003e\u003cbr /\u003eThe result was an \u003cstrong\u003eunrivaled catalogue of all known genera of the palm family\u003c/strong\u003e, outlining the modern classification of palms, describing all the palms of Brazil, and producing the \u003cstrong\u003efirst maps of palm biogeography\u003c/strong\u003e. Von Martius’s folio is unusual in its inclusion of cross-sectioned diagrams, conveying the architecture of these mighty trees, which central Europeans would have found hard to imagine accurately. For all their ethereal charms, his compositions were often rich and complex in their references. They wove together not only colors and forms, but also his Jewish roots with his present encounters in Paris, markers of faith with gestures of love and symbols of hope with testimonies of trauma.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAcross scenes of birth, love, marriage, and death, this dependable artist introduction explores the many versions of Chagall's rich vocabulary. with the launch of Weird Tales magazine, was reinvigorated in the 1960s with The Lord of the Rings, Conan the Barbarian paperbacks with Frank Frazetta covers, and the late '60s emergence of fantasy psychedelia. It went big in the '70s with the role-playing game Dungeons \u0026amp; Dragons, the brilliant French magazine Metal Hurlant, and the first Star Wars film. The number of active artists peaked in that decade, but a new generation of fans discovered the genre through fantasy trading card games in the '90s, leading to a massive interest in the art form today. Frank Frazetta's oil paintings-when they infrequently come to market-have sold for more than $ 5 million in recent years. Thông qua các bản trải nghiệm đầy đủ và các chi tiết được sắp xếp cẩn thận, chúng ta khám phá toàn bộ phạm vi tiếp cận và những phát minh hấp dẫn của thiên tài nghệ sĩ cũng như trí tưởng tượng đáng kinh ngạc.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOnly 20 paintings and eight drawings are confidently assigned to Netherlandish painter Hieronymus Bosch (c. 1450-1516) but in their fantastical visions they have secured his place as one of the most cult artists in history. 500 years on from his death, his works continue to inspire scholars, artists, designers, and musicians, death metal band names and designer dresses.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis edition offers the complete and haunting Bosch world in one compact format. Through full spreads and carefully curated details, we explore the full reach and compelling inventions of the artist's genius as well as disturbing imagination. We encounter his hybrid creatures, his nightmarish scenarios, his religious and moral framework, and his pictorial versions of contemporary proverbs and idioms. Along the way, art historian and Bosch expert Stefan Fischer reveals the most important themes and influences in these cryptic, mesmerizing masterpieces.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAbout the series\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTASCHEN is 40!
